[ACTION] north [STATE] Dormitory Dozens of openings line the hall, each leading to a separate cell, except for the west, which leads to the cloister. [ACTION] west [STATE] Cloister In the warmer months, Brother Matteo maintains a beautiful garden in the cloister. Now there is nothing but a few dead vines sticking out from beneath a blanket of snow. Still, it has a calm dignity: the wind finds no entrance here.
